Furthermore, if there is one opponent who is not giving up, deals 28% x 4 and 84% x 8 damage to a single opponent instead.\n[Effects obtained when you consume MPs more than one activation] Every 5 additional MPs increase, your own Damage increases by 2% and {{D}} decreases by 2% (3 turns). Also, if you consume 40 additional MPs, there is a high probability that the opponent's {{C}} (high) is reduced (1 turn) if you consume 80 additional MPs, you will be in {{A}} state (99 turns)\n*The effects obtained when you consume more than one MP, each is counted and multiple activations will also occur.
